<h2 class='date-header'><span>Thursday, January 9, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RkdC9R-A87M/Us_0FdxT1cI/AAAAAAAAGh4/RDGxzUtToUg/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-08.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='4388504906915444063' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='3671999814058158459' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='3671999814058158459'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2014/01/event-update-for-2014-01-08.html'>Event Update For 2014-01-08</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3671999814058158459' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RkdC9R-A87M/Us_0FdxT1cI/AAAAAAAAGh4/RDGxzUtToUg/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-08.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RkdC9R-A87M/Us_0FdxT1cI/AAAAAAAAGh4/RDGxzUtToUg/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-08.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-s5I2oErUk5I/Us_0LNE_NgI/AAAAAAAAGiA/8YSZJ_wEQ04/s1600/H2S_SkullTalk_2014_01_08_ItsOurDoodie.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-s5I2oErUk5I/Us_0LNE_NgI/AAAAAAAAGiA/8YSZJ_wEQ04/s1600/H2S_SkullTalk_2014_01_08_ItsOurDoodie.jpg" /></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-I2MojdnLkXM/UXkSCL6HP8I/AAAAAAAACYU/JrdSTb1lFlQ/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_FullHypothesis.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-I2MojdnLkXM/UXkSCL6HP8I/AAAAAAAACYU/JrdSTb1lFlQ/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_FullHypothesis.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<br />
<br />
<div style="text-align: left;">
<a href="http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2012/02/jumping-jack-flash-hypothesis-its-gas.html">http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2012/02/jumping-jack-flash-hypothesis-its-gas.html</a>
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Yo-QFpngGvs/UXkSPLQ0UYI/AAAAAAAACYc/GYaUmcmg1f4/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SummaryOfHypothesis.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Yo-QFpngGvs/UXkSPLQ0UYI/AAAAAAAACYc/GYaUmcmg1f4/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SummaryOfHypothesis.jpg" /></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
The seas, lakes and oceans are now pluming deadly hydrogen sulfide and suffocating methane. Hydrogen sulfide is a highly toxic water-soluble heavier-than-air gas and will accumulate in low-lying areas. Methane is slightly more buoyant than normal air and so will be all around, but will tend to contaminate our atmosphere from the top down. These gases are sickening and killing oxygen-using life all around the world, including human life, as our atmosphere is increasingly poisoned. Because both gases are highly flammable and because our entire civilization is built around fire and flammable fuels, this is leading to more fires and explosions. This is an extinction level event and will likely decimate both the biosphere and human population and it is debatable whether humankind can survive this event.
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q9POfIMUgcI/UXkSaEaSfgI/AAAAAAAACYk/YotoGzFOwIY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q9POfIMUgcI/UXkSaEaSfgI/AAAAAAAACYk/YotoGzFOwIY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<br />
<div style="text-align: left;">
<br />
A. More fires and more explosions, especially along the coasts, but everywhere generally.<br />
B. Many more animal die-offs, of all kinds, and especially oceanic species.<br />
C. More multiples of people will be found dead in their homes, as if they'd dropped dead.<br />
D. More corpses found in low-lying areas, all over the world.<br />
E. More unusual vehicular accidents.<br />
F. Improved unemployment numbers as people die off.
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-two_ua-yeDA/UXkTA_N6DZI/AAAAAAAACYs/Hc1nxNTOrZY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SpotlightStory.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-two_ua-yeDA/UXkTA_N6DZI/AAAAAAAACYs/Hc1nxNTOrZY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SpotlightStory.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<strong>Category: Fires And Explosions</strong></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">

<a href="http://www.nj.com/somerset/index.ssf/2014/01/branchburg_no_threat_from_big_fire_burning_oil_at_pseg_station_on_route_202.html">http://www.nj.com/somerset/index.ssf/2014/01/branchburg_no_threat_from_big_fire_burning_oil_at_pseg_station_on_route_202.html</a><br />
<a href="http://abclocal.go.com/wabc/story?section=news/local/new_jersey&amp;id=9386428">http://abclocal.go.com/wabc/story?section=news/local/new_jersey&amp;id=9386428</a><br />
<a href="http://www.mycentraljersey.com/article/20140108/NJNEWS14/301080040/Fire-closes-Route-202-in-Branchburg">http://www.mycentraljersey.com/article/20140108/NJNEWS14/301080040/Fire-closes-Route-202-in-Branchburg</a><br />

2014-01-08 - <strong>Electrical room erupts in flame at school</strong> in Winston-Salem (North Carolina):</div>
<a href="http://www.journalnow.com/news/local/article_2d3e2850-78dc-11e3-9d62-001a4bcf6878.html">http://www.journalnow.com/news/local/article_2d3e2850-78dc-11e3-9d62-001a4bcf6878.html</a><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<em><strong>Note:</strong> More electrified copper igniting. Hydrogen sulfide is reactive with copper, especially electrified copper. The US gubment has trained for a widespread grid failure, and this is why. Oh sure, that'd be useful in the event that we get hit by an EMP or solar flare too, but those are just <strong>possibilities</strong> - this copper reactivity problem is <strong>ongoing</strong>. It's actually <strong>worse</strong> than an EMP or solar flare too. An EMP would hit a geographic region. A solar flare might hit half the planet. Atmospheric contamination will affect the ENTIRE planet, and it'll just continue to worsen, likely for thousands of years. Living humans will have long since abandoned the surface of the Earth by then though, either voluntarily by relocating, or involuntarily by dying...</em></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<em></em>&nbsp;</div>

<a href="http://abclocal.go.com/wls/story?section=news/local/wisconsin&amp;id=9387319">http://abclocal.go.com/wls/story?section=news/local/wisconsin&amp;id=9387319</a><br />
<a href="http://journaltimes.com/news/state-and-regional/explosion-like-sounds-rattle-residents/article_515ee9a2-6026-5055-8107-30c6bdc2eeba.html">http://journaltimes.com/news/state-and-regional/explosion-like-sounds-rattle-residents/article_515ee9a2-6026-5055-8107-30c6bdc2eeba.html</a><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "The series of explosion-like sounds rattled residents from Waupun, Campbellsport and elsewhere Tuesday and sent Fond du Lac County sheriff&#8217;s deputies out looking for a cause. Geologists say the booms were likely a phenomenon commonly known as an ice quake. It&#8217;s caused by water that sinks into the soil and bedrock where it freezes and expands, causing an explosive popping sound that feels like a mild earthquake."</em><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Note:</strong> That'd almost sound believable, except these mysterious explosions didn't happen like this in previous years, and it was also happening in the spring, summer and fall when there were no freezing temps. Also, some of these mysterious explosions are accompanied by a 'flash of light' in the sky, and this 'ice quake' story doesn't even begin to explain that...</em><br />
<br />
2014-01-08 - <strong>Explosion and fire hits biotech business</strong> in <strong>coastal</strong> San Francisco (California), 2 injured:<br />

<a href="http://abclocal.go.com/kgo/story?section=news/local/peninsula&amp;id=9386707">http://abclocal.go.com/kgo/story?section=news/local/peninsula&amp;id=9386707</a><br />
<a href="http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/01/09/us-usa-lab-explosion-idUSBREA0801D20140109">http://www.reuters.com/article/2014/01/09/us-usa-lab-explosion-idUSBREA0801D20140109</a><br />

<a href="http://www.news24.com/Africa/News/Tanker-crash-fire-kills-15-in-Lagos-20140108">http://www.news24.com/Africa/News/Tanker-crash-fire-kills-15-in-Lagos-20140108</a><br />
<a href="http://www.nation.co.ke/news/africa/Tanker-crash-fire-kills-15-in-Lagos-rescue-agency/-/1066/2139560/-/h7kstq/-/index.html">http://www.nation.co.ke/news/africa/Tanker-crash-fire-kills-15-in-Lagos-rescue-agency/-/1066/2139560/-/h7kstq/-/index.html</a><br />
<a href="http://tribune.com.ng/news2013/index.php/en/news/lead-stories/item/30441-12-feared-dead-in-lagos-tanker-fire-accident-%E2%80%A25-houses,-15-vehicles-razed.html">http://tribune.com.ng/news2013/index.php/en/news/lead-stories/item/30441-12-feared-dead-in-lagos-tanker-fire-accident-%E2%80%A25-houses,-15-vehicles-razed.html</a><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "A trader at the spare parts market, who simply identified himself as Onyema, told the Nigerian Tribune that the truck was coming from Kirikiri when it had <strong>brake failure</strong>, while efforts by the driver to halt its movement caused it to tumble."</em><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "A branch of a bank in the area, four buildings and about 15 vehicles were completely burnt, while three other houses were partly burnt in the inferno."</em><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Note:</strong> Another brake failure in a massive vehicle. Tires and brake pads are absorbing hydrogen sulfide. Then when brakes are applied, an unusual amount of heat is generated, because hydrogen sulfide burns very hot. Then bad things can happen: tires ignite or explode, <strong>brakes burn out</strong> or ignite, fluid lines rupture, the entire vehicle goes up in flames, or all of the above. This problem hits massive vehicles the worst - like <strong>tanker trucks</strong>, tractor trailers, dump trucks, buses, big RVs, etc - but no vehicle is immune...</em><br />
<br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>Wednesday, January 8, 2014</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry' itemprop='blogPost' itemscope='itemscope' itemtype='http://schema.org/BlogPosting'>
<meta content='http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oNvAulf9Lwo/Us6if5tig3I/AAAAAAAAGhc/r2S9VzwJxW0/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-07.jpg' itemprop='image_url'/>
<meta content='4388504906915444063' itemprop='blogId'/>
<meta content='5760244646755872484' itemprop='postId'/>
<a name='5760244646755872484'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title' itemprop='name'>
<a href='http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2014/01/event-update-for-2014-01-07.html'>Event Update For 2014-01-07</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-5760244646755872484' itemprop='articleBody'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oNvAulf9Lwo/Us6if5tig3I/AAAAAAAAGhc/r2S9VzwJxW0/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-07.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-oNvAulf9Lwo/Us6if5tig3I/AAAAAAAAGhc/r2S9VzwJxW0/s1600/H2S_Update_2014-01-07.jpg" /></a></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tbZ4xAkF3zQ/Us6il4AC8fI/AAAAAAAAGhk/cbJkwORaPWQ/s1600/H2S_SkullTalk_2014_01_07_DawnOfTheDead.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-tbZ4xAkF3zQ/Us6il4AC8fI/AAAAAAAAGhk/cbJkwORaPWQ/s1600/H2S_SkullTalk_2014_01_07_DawnOfTheDead.jpg" /></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-I2MojdnLkXM/UXkSCL6HP8I/AAAAAAAACYU/JrdSTb1lFlQ/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_FullHypothesis.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-I2MojdnLkXM/UXkSCL6HP8I/AAAAAAAACYU/JrdSTb1lFlQ/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_FullHypothesis.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<br />
<br />
<div style="text-align: left;">
<a href="http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2012/02/jumping-jack-flash-hypothesis-its-gas.html">http://jumpingjackflashhypothesis.blogspot.com/2012/02/jumping-jack-flash-hypothesis-its-gas.html</a>
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Yo-QFpngGvs/UXkSPLQ0UYI/AAAAAAAACYc/GYaUmcmg1f4/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SummaryOfHypothesis.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Yo-QFpngGvs/UXkSPLQ0UYI/AAAAAAAACYc/GYaUmcmg1f4/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SummaryOfHypothesis.jpg" /></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
The seas, lakes and oceans are now pluming deadly hydrogen sulfide and suffocating methane. Hydrogen sulfide is a highly toxic water-soluble heavier-than-air gas and will accumulate in low-lying areas. Methane is slightly more buoyant than normal air and so will be all around, but will tend to contaminate our atmosphere from the top down. These gases are sickening and killing oxygen-using life all around the world, including human life, as our atmosphere is increasingly poisoned. Because both gases are highly flammable and because our entire civilization is built around fire and flammable fuels, this is leading to more fires and explosions. This is an extinction level event and will likely decimate both the biosphere and human population and it is debatable whether humankind can survive this event.
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q9POfIMUgcI/UXkSaEaSfgI/AAAAAAAACYk/YotoGzFOwIY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Q9POfIMUgcI/UXkSaEaSfgI/AAAAAAAACYk/YotoGzFOwIY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<br />
<div style="text-align: left;">
<br />
A. More fires and more explosions, especially along the coasts, but everywhere generally.<br />
B. Many more animal die-offs, of all kinds, and especially oceanic species.<br />
C. More multiples of people will be found dead in their homes, as if they'd dropped dead.<br />
D. More corpses found in low-lying areas, all over the world.<br />
E. More unusual vehicular accidents.<br />
F. Improved unemployment numbers as people die off.
</div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-two_ua-yeDA/UXkTA_N6DZI/AAAAAAAACYs/Hc1nxNTOrZY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SpotlightStory.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-two_ua-yeDA/UXkTA_N6DZI/AAAAAAAACYs/Hc1nxNTOrZY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_SpotlightStory.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<strong>Category: Fires And Explosions</strong></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">

<a href="http://poetsareangels.com/2014/01/08/parts-of-salem-closed-after-multiple-manhole-covers-explode/">http://poetsareangels.com/2014/01/08/parts-of-salem-closed-after-multiple-manhole-covers-explode/</a><br />

<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<em><strong>Note:</strong> Yep, that stench is at least in part hydrogen sulfide, and it is poisoning the people nearby. It's not at high enough levels to just outright knock the whole city dead (yet), else they would lose their ability to smell it because of olfactory paralysis, but they may experience long-term health issues like neurological problems, heart problems, kidney problems...</em></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">

<a href="http://www.telegraphindia.com/1140108/jsp/jharkhand/story_17761227.jsp">http://www.telegraphindia.com/1140108/jsp/jharkhand/story_17761227.jsp</a><br />
<a href="http://www.topix.com/in/dhanbad/2014/01/fire-in-katras-19-families-displaced">http://www.topix.com/in/dhanbad/2014/01/fire-in-katras-19-families-displaced</a><br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<em><strong>Note:</strong> Hydrogen sulfide is a heavier-than-air gas and it will tend to seek out low-lying areas, like <strong>underground</strong> areas and facilities. It's also extremely flammable, much more flammable than natural gas or methane, and because it is so reactive with so many different things it will ignite very easily, causing fires and explosions. These underground fires and explosions are clearly escalating...</em></div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
<em></em>&nbsp;</div>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BLvS4TufWRM/UXkTM3ZQPuI/AAAAAAAACY0/EUBQZeR0MPY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions_FiresExplosions.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-BLvS4TufWRM/UXkTM3ZQPuI/AAAAAAAACY0/EUBQZeR0MPY/s1600/H2S_UpdateBands_Predictions_FiresExplosions.jpg" /></a>

2014-01-07 - <strong>Mysterious explosions shake homes and rattle residents</strong> in Colonial Heights (Virginia):<br />
<a href="http://hisz.rsoe.hu/alertmap/site/?pageid=event_desc&amp;edis_id=UEV-20140108-42205-USA">http://hisz.rsoe.hu/alertmap/site/?pageid=event_desc&amp;edis_id=UEV-20140108-42205-USA</a><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "Some call them booms while others referred to them as explosions. Some said the noises were so intense that they rattled their homes. 'It's a loud, loud boom,' Clint Lanier, who lives in Chesterfield County, told CBS 6 senior reporter Wayne Covil. 'It ain't no shotgun and it ain't no kind of gun. It's like an explosion.' Sgt. Rob Ruxer with Colonial Heights police said dispatchers received at least three calls just before 5:30 p.m. Sunday from citizens in separate areas of the city about a loud noise."</em><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Note:</strong> This is sort of a coastal city. The James <strong>River</strong> goes inland from the <strong>coast</strong> and hits Colonial Heights, and then turns into the Appomattox <strong>River</strong>, with Colonial Heights located where the two rivers meet. These mysterious explosions really started escalating around the world a couple of years ago, right as methane began seriously spewing into the atmosphere, and right as events involving 'rotten egg' odors began escalating. Not a coincidence. Both methane and hydrogen sulfide are explosively flammable and as the atmospheric contamination intensifies, more fires and explosions are to be expected. Eventually these explosions may rival the small nuclear explosion that destroyed Hiroshima, but minus the radiation, unless an explosion takes out a nuclear plant, many of which are located on <strong>coasts </strong>and <strong>all</strong> of which are near <strong>bodies of water</strong> for cooling...</em><br />

<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "A Canadian National Railway train carrying propane and crude oil derailed and caught fire on Tuesday in northwest New Brunswick, Canada, the <strong>latest</strong> in a <strong>string of train accidents</strong> that have put the surging crude-by-rail business under heavy scrutiny. No one was injured but about 45 nearby homes were evacuated when the train derailed near the village of Plaster Rock at about 7 p.m. local time (2300 GMT), local officials and the railroad said."</em><br />

2014-01-07 - <strong>Deadly cold wave freezes the crap out of the United States</strong>, 21 killed:<br />
<a href="http://hisz.rsoe.hu/alertmap/site/?pageid=event_desc&amp;edis_id=CW-20140109-42214-USA">http://hisz.rsoe.hu/alertmap/site/?pageid=event_desc&amp;edis_id=CW-20140109-42214-USA</a><br />
<br />
<em><strong>Quote:</strong> "The air flow resulted in the breaking of numerous weather records, creating the coldest Jan. 7 ever recorded in Cleveland (minus 11 degrees Fahrenheit), Atlanta (6 degrees) and Austin, Texas (12 degrees), NBC News said. When accounting for wind chill, some northern cities saw punishing conditions of minus 16 in New York City, minus 31 in Chicago, and minus 45 in northernmost Minnesota, according to NBC. All of these were <strong>colder</strong> than the Tuesday morning reading of minus 6 recorded at the <strong>South Pole</strong>..."</em><br />
